 North East Delhi Lok Sabha seat: AAP, a triangular contest between Congress and BJP, is a Lok Sabha seat in the North East Delhi National Capital Region
 uttar purvi dilli main 2009 main pehla loksabhaa (saamaanya) chunaav ladaa gaya
 It is located in Delhi district, which was established in 1997
 is seat par philhal bijepi kaa kabja he
 But in the coming 2019 Lok Sabha elections, one can see a triangular contest between Congress, Aam Aadmi Party and BJP here
 aam aadmi party (aap)ne loksabhaa chunaav 2019 ke liye yahaan se dilip pandey ke naam kii ghoshnaa kar di he
 Political Background The 10 assembly constituencies included in North East Delhi Lok Sabha seat are Burari, Rohtash Nagar, Babarpur, Timarpur, Seelampur, Gokalpur, Seemapuri, Ghonda, Mustafabad and Karwal Nagar
 inamen se simapuri or gokalpur ke kshetra anusuchit jati ke ummidavaaron ke liye arakshit hai
 The North East Delhi constituency is one of the most populous areas of Delhi with a population of 2,241,624 people according to the 2011 Census of India
 saamaajik taana-banabharat nirvachan ayog 2009 ke aankadon ke mutabik, uttar purvi dilli loksabhaa nirvachan kshetra (nirvachan kshetra sankhya 2) main kul matadaataaon kii sankhya 1,677,058 he, inamen se 931,142 purush hai or 745,916 mahilaayein hai
 The economy of the region depends on industries, agricultural production
 yahaan se sansad ke vartmaan seating sadsy bijepi ke manoj tiwari hai

 voton kaa pattern bataata he ki yah chunaav kisi bhi party ke liye aasaan nahin tha

 is jeet se bijepi ko dilli main kaaphi takat mili

 The doctors said during their protest, 'we are opposing the NMC bill
 is bill ko puri tarah se hataaya janaa chahie

 'kendriya mantrimandal ne is vidheyak ko 17 july ke din manjuuri de di thi
 The main objective of the Bill is to establish a Medical Commission in place of Medical Council of India (MCI)
 bataaya jaataa he ki isse bhartiya chikitsa parishad adhinium 1956 nirast ho jayega
 The Medical Commission will regulate all fees for 50 per cent seats in private medical colleges and deemed universities
 jisase pravesh shulk main kami kii ummid jataai ja rahi he
 Why is there a ruckus on this bill? Under the 32nd provision of the National Medical Bill, Community Health Providers will get a license to prescribe medicines and treat patients
 jabaki is par doctoron ko aapatti he kyonki isse marijon kii jaan khatre main pad jaaegi

 jabaki doctoron kaa kahana he ki isse neem-hakim or jholachhap doctoron ko badhaava milegaa

 jabaki doctoron kaa kahana he ki isse privet medical collejon main bhrashtachar ko badhaava milegaa

 Finance Minister Pranab Mukherjee has said that the country's gross domestic product (GDP) growth rate of 8 in the current financial year
 5 pratishat rahegi
 However, at the same time he expressed concern over the country's agricultural sector, saying that to maintain the high rate of GDP, it is necessary that the growth rate of agriculture sector is four percent per annum
 vitt mantri ne ek tivi channel kaarykram ke dauraan kaha, is baat kii kaaphi sambhaavna he ki ham 2010-11 main 8
 Will be able to achieve economic growth rate of 5 percent
  yah puche jane par ki kya bharat kii aarthik vruddhi apane bharose aage bad sakati he yaa phir use sarkaar ke protsaahan kii jarurat he, mukherjee ne kaha, nishchit taur par krishi kshetra mahatvapurn he
 Mukherjee said that the growth rate of industrial production has reached ten percent, while the services sector is also contributing to the growth
 unhone kaha ki krishi kshetra chintaa kaa kaaran he
 To achieve high economic growth rate of 9 percent, it is necessary that the growth rate of agriculture sector should remain constant at four percent for long period
 yah puche jane par ki kya vah rajkoshiya ghate ko kam karne ke lakshya ko hasil kar paaenge, mukherjee ne kaha, mujhe puraa bharosa he ki main 5
 Will be able to achieve the level of 5 percent
 vitt mantri ne kaha ki rajkoshiya sthiti ko majboot karnaa meri sabase badi praathamikta he
 Also maintaining high growth rate
 main nahin chaahunga ki rajkoshiya sthiti ko kamjor karne kii evaj main vruddhi hasil kii jaae

 vahiin sirf 3ji spectrum kii nilaamee se hi sarkaar ko 67,000 karod rupee se adhik kaa rajasav mil gaya he

 According to the Meteorological Department, in the next 4-5 days, day temperatures in Punjab, Haryana, Rajasthan, Madhya Pradesh, Maharashtra and Gujarat will go up by 4  C
 is samay gujarat or pashchimi rajasthan ke zyaadaatar ilaakon main taapmaana saamaanya ke mukaable 5 degree celsius upar bana hua he
 Day temperatures in many areas are around 43 to 44 degrees Celsius here
 mausam vibhaag ke mutabikane vaale dinon main uttar bharat ke tamaam ilaakon main hawa kii dasha or disha badal jaaegi or is vajah se din ke taapmaana upar chadh jaaenge
 There is a big reason behind this, at this time a weak Western disturbance has reached over Jammu and Kashmir and due to this, mercury started climbing in all areas of North India including Delhi
 mausam vibhaag ke diarector charan singh ke mutabik uttar bharat, pashchim bharat or madhya bharat main kai ilaakon main hitwave banane kii ashanka bad gai he
 According to weather experts, the possibility of increasing heat in northern India has increased because of the possibility of cyclone in the Bay of Bengal
 is samay
 a low pressure area has formed near Andaman and Nicobar and this area will become more powerful in the next 48 to 72 hours
 aisi sambhaavna he ki 15 april ke baad ye wedar system cyclone main tabdeel ho jaaegein
 After converting into a cyclone, this weather system will move towards Myanmar and its residual residue may cause another cyclone after landfall there
 in sambhaavnaaon ke chalate mausam vibhaag puure ghatnakram par baarik najar banaae hue he
 Weather models of supercomputers are currently predicting cyclones, but there is a possibility of change in this situation, so the meteorological department is avoiding speaking clearly about this

 is cell kaa kaam transgenderon ke khilaaf hinsa, utpeedan, bhedbhaav kii shikayaton ko dekhnaa or transgender samaaj ke liye jaagrukta paidaa karnaa hoga
 On June 29, Swati Maliwal, chairperson of the Delhi Women's Commission met Promila Gupta, a member of the Commission, along with several people from the transgender society and tried to understand the problems facing her
